Evolution of Additional Grain Tax in Jiangsu Province 129

According to a certain gentleman yesterday, the case of adding two yuan per stone to the winter grain tax in Jiangsu Province originated in the Sun Chuanfang era and was called "borrowed grain," with the expectation of repayment. It was collected for another year in the 17th year and renamed the "Northern Expedition Donation," with the intention of abolishing it after the success of the Northern Expedition. Therefore, it was suspended for one year in the 18th year. Unexpectedly, in the 19th year, the Jiangsu Provincial Government submitted a request to the Executive Yuan to continue the collection indefinitely. Due to local opposition, it was changed to one year at a time, and it was no longer continued. In the 20th and 21st years, the provincial government again persuaded the Ministry of Finance and obtained approval to continue the collection. However, the Ministry of Finance ultimately disagreed. Now, Chairman Gu is again discussing with the Ministry of Finance to extend the collection period, but no decision has been made. It has been found that the tax burden of our province is the heaviest in the country. At this time of rural decline and economic hardship, if this additional and harsh levy is not stopped, the bankruptcy of farmers will endanger the foundation of the country, which is truly worrying.

Deep Disappointment of the Frozen Fish Merchants Regarding the Fisheries Bureau's Handling of Ocean Protection 130

Optimism Uncertain About Future Construction Funds

Since the Ministry of Industry began collecting fisheries construction fees, various fresh and salted fish merchants have risen up in opposition. Although Mr. Yu Qiaqing, Du Yuesheng, and Yu Zuoting have repeatedly mediated, some of the fish merchants are still unwilling to comply. Among them, only the frozen fish merchants have been paying the construction fees as required for the past four months without objection, due to the ocean protection. Recently, due to the sinking of the Fuhai patrol ship and the withdrawal of the Qing'an, only the old ship Haiying is available, and it has not been repaired. Moreover, the Haihong and Haigu ships cannot sail to the distant seas. The Fisheries Bureau has no active remedial measures for this. Furthermore, there are more pirates this year, in addition to the Taiwanese bandits, there are also hundreds of Zhu Songzhou's troops scattered around Xiaoyangshan, all fully armed, causing even more harm. The various frozen fish merchants are deeply disappointed with the Fisheries Bureau's handling of ocean protection. The bureau often touts active construction, but even this minimum level of ocean protection cannot meet the merchants' demands, let alone anything else. Therefore, they have recently gathered to discuss joining the opposition, so the future of the construction fees is still uncertain.

Reduced Price for Urgent Telegrams Sent to Alaska via Radio 131

Reduced by Eight Yuan and Eight Jiao Per Word

It has been found that the fee for urgent telegrams sent from our country to Alaska has been ten yuan and three jiao per word. According to the International Telegraph Bureau in this city, starting from the 16th of this month, all such telegrams transmitted by radio and marked [via International Station and Consortium] will be reduced by eight yuan and eight jiao per word. The bureau has already notified all telegraph offices and radio stations of this.

Rebuttal by the Miscellaneous Grain Industry Association, etc., Regarding Pan Xulun's Opinion on Partnership Liability 132

Based on Commercial Practices, Supporting Evidence from Laws of Various Countries

The Provision for Joint and Several Liability Should Be Abolished Immediately

The Shanghai Municipal Miscellaneous Grain, Oil Cake Industry Six Trade Associations sent a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce rebutting accountant Pan Xulun's opinion on partnership liability. The original letter stated: "We respectfully submit that after reading the reports on the 25th and 26th of July, Accountant Pan Xulun's opinion on partnership liability, regarding the partnership itself, cited four malpractices and three difficulties regarding legal provisions, and finally ended with three reasons. In summary, [he opposes changing partnership liability to be shared according to shares, and advocates adding provisions for unlimited liability companies with shared responsibility in the Company Law]. Our associations, etc., consider this a matter of vital interest and dare not agree. Therefore, we do not fear being tedious and will re-examine the established rules and seek new examples, and slightly correct Mr. Pan's opinion. Please consider it accordingly."

Legal Action 133

(1) Accountant Pan Xulun opposes changing partnership liability to be shared according to shares, and the first reason is that "[the partnership organization is legally only a contractual relationship between partners internally, and has no independent name or legal personality externally, so it cannot be the subject of litigation...]". According to the meaning of partnership, it refers to a contract where two or more people invest to operate a common business. The partnership stipulated in the Civil Code originally belongs to a contractual act. Except for undisclosed partnerships, the establishment of any partnership contract, even if it cannot be said to belong entirely to commercial acts, ordinary operations of common businesses are mostly commercial. It can always be considered a commercial act. Since it belongs to a commercial act, the registration of the trade name and the registration of the business, even if judged from the original intent of our country's legislation, cannot be said to have no independent name or legal personality. Since the partnership organization is a legal organization in accordance with civil law regulations, its partnership contract is also one of the legal acts. If litigation occurs, it can of course be recognized as the subject of rights and obligations in law. The judgment in the third year, Upper Character No. 40, states, "[...]In ordinary partnerships, all general partners are the subject of rights and obligations". From this, it is clear that the reasons relied upon by Accountant Pan Xulun are not legal or reasonable.

Business Registration 134

(2) Accountant Pan Xulun opposes changing partnership liability to be shared according to shares, and the second reason is that "[the establishment of a partnership has no obligation to apply for registration with the competent authority, and there is no basis for partnership bankruptcy...]". This second reason follows the fallacies of the first reason mentioned above, still believing that because there is no registration or registration, the disadvantage lies in the difficulty for creditors to investigate. Regarding this point, it has long been stipulated in the current merchant precedents, and if it can be strictly implemented, there will be no way to keep it secret. Judging from the current facts, your association has already clearly stipulated regulations for business registration and submitted them to the competent authority for implementation, so there is no need to worry about it.

Unlimited Liability Company 135

(3) Accountant Pan Xulun advocates adding provisions for unlimited liability companies with shared responsibility in the Company Law, and his opinion is that "[...]But because a partnership contract cannot have legal personality, only a company has this qualification, so the organization of shared unlimited liability should be stipulated in the Company Law...]". It must be known that in civilized legal systems, business is free and there are no restrictions on the qualifications of merchants. The partnership contract stipulated in our country's Civil Code is based on liberalism as the norm. Therefore, anyone who has the ability to enter into a contract and independently bear obligations can be a merchant and engage in commerce. This is the principle adopted in legislation, which is very suitable for the national conditions of our country. A company must follow a certain system. It is not enough to simply have two or more people partnering to operate a business to be recklessly called a company. If the requirements stipulated in the Company Law are not followed, such as the fixed number of people, the signing of articles of association in writing, and registration with the government, then the benefits protected by the Company Law cannot be obtained. This is a kind of absolute mandatory principle. In the last two or three decades, the organization of shops in our country, new-style joint ventures in major trading ports, have sometimes adopted the company system, while the rest are partnership organizations. The history is very long and the customs have become widespread. In order to implement the proposal to stipulate the organization of shared unlimited liability in the Company Law, Accountant Pan Xulun does not hesitate to forcibly associate partnership business with company organization and discuss them as one. He directly wants to turn this free commercial example into a purely mandatory regulation, which is like cutting one's feet to fit the shoes, not in line with custom, not suitable for national conditions. In terms of legal principles, it is a misunderstanding. In terms of malpractices, it is truly enough to disrupt the original stability of society.

Laws of Various Countries 136

(4) Accountant Pan Xulun, regarding our associations' request to amend Article 681 of the Civil Code, which stipulates joint and several liability for partnership debts, to be shared according to shares, raised three difficulties. The most important of these is that "[In all countries of the world, all partners are jointly and severally liable, and our country's legal system should not be unique]". Accountant Pan Xulun made this affirmative statement, but it is not known what basis he has. Except for the United Kingdom and the United States, which have no codified laws that can be used as reference, please cite the explicit legal provisions regarding partnership debts in the laws of France, Japan, Switzerland, and Germany and translate them below as rebuttal evidence: 1. Article 1862 of the French Civil Code: "In partnerships not established for commercial purposes, the partners are not jointly and severally liable for the obligations of the partnership. One partner may not make his other partners assume his obligations, except when there are special provisions for the other partners to jointly and severally assume the obligations of one person." 2. Article 675 of the Japanese Civil Code: "If the creditor of the partnership does not know the standard for loss sharing among the partners at the time the debt arises, he may exercise his rights against each partner in an equal portion (i.e., the average portion)." 3. Article 977 of the entire Swiss Civil Code: "There are no regulations regarding responsibility for partnership contracts." (Note: According to Article 1, Paragraph 2 of its Civil Code, regarding legal issues, verbally or interpretively, judicial officials can even base their judgments or applications on established academic theories and precedents of judgments.) 4. Article 725 of the German Civil Code: "When the partnership property is insufficient to pay off common debts and repay shares, the partners shall supplement the insufficient amount according to the pro rata share of loss distribution." Judging from the above examples of legal provisions in various national civil codes, the affirmative statement of Accountant Pan Xulun that "[In all countries of the world, all partners are jointly and severally liable]", it is worth considering whether there is a legal basis for the argument [against changing partnership liability to be shared according to shares]. Furthermore, when a country enacts laws, if it is not based on its own inherent customs, it must be based on the codified laws or precedents of its advanced countries to stipulate regulations and make them legal codes to bind the people. Now, let us first talk about the purpose of legislation in our country. The Civil Code promulgated in our country, at the time of its legislation, apart from the United Kingdom and the United States, which had no codified laws that could be used as reference and were completely incompatible with our country's national conditions and commercial customs, was mostly based on European countries with codified laws and referred to our country's historical customs before starting to compile. All three laws of the General Provisions, Obligations, and Property Rights of the Civil Code either took the law from Germany or even took the legislative examples of the Swiss and Japanese Civil Codes. Based on this, exploring the legislative intent of our country's Civil Code, it is not difficult to see everything, and the legislative system can be found. Secondly, let us talk about the customs of partnership business in our country. The organizational regulations of partnership business in our country must first mutually agree on a list (i.e., a contract). The common rules stipulated on the list, regardless of whether they are for the whole country or any region, are generally recognized. Profits are shared equally according to shares, and losses are shared according to shares. They have been passed down for thousands of years and have long become a common practice in the business world. Accountant Pan Xulun is also concerned about business people, so he should have a deep understanding of this inherent custom. Observing the above-mentioned civil law examples of France, Japan, Switzerland, and Germany, as well as the legislative intent of our country at that time and the inherent customs of the country, considering Article 681 of the Civil Code, which stipulates that partners are jointly and severally liable for partnership debts, is it not completely contrary? If, as Accountant Pan Xulun said, "[Our country's legal system should not be unique]", then for the amendment of this legal example, we should all express sympathy and work together to promote it. Why hold a dissenting opinion and openly oppose it? Our associations, etc., are truly filled with regret.

Legislative Spirit 137

(5) Accountant Pan Xulun cited four malpractices, one being, "[Wouldn't the protection of creditors be completely lost?]", another being, "[The harm to creditors is immeasurable]", a third being, "[The creditor's side is almost without any protection]", and a fourth being, "[It is tantamount to losing most of the existing guarantees originally set for each creditor]". Looking at the entire text, it is everywhere thinking for the creditors, without mentioning a single word about the debtors. It must be known that debtors are often in the position of economically weak parties. If the law is always based on protecting creditors, wouldn't the legislative spirit be completely lost? The introduction to the Obligations section of the Civil Code says, "[Our country's current legislation is based on the public interest of the entire society and is always based on seeking public happiness. This is the way of the king, and the spirit of benevolence, forgiveness, and fairness should permeate the entire Civil Code, protecting the weak everywhere]". It also says, "The Obligations section of the Civil Code was originally called the Creditor's section, but now it has been changed to the Obligations section because the word creditor, from the perspective of the name, seems to imply that that law is specifically to protect creditors. Specifically protecting creditors is the way of the hegemon". Based on this, Accountant Pan Xulun's view of actively protecting creditors cannot but be regarded as a subjective error. Based on this subjective view, the so-called malpractices, so-called difficulties, and so-called reasons are all inconsistent with objective facts and go without saying.

Violation of Contract 138

In summary, the civil laws of various countries mentioned above, which served as the basic laws when our country formulated the Civil Code, have no provisions for partners being jointly and severally liable. Originally, partnership behavior is contractual behavior, so regardless of whether it is commercial or non-commercial, regarding losses, it must be shared according to the contract agreed upon by each partner. This is the greatest principle of the Civil Code's contract law regulations and must not be equated with the unlimited liability shareholders stipulated in the Company Law, who also bear this unlimited liability. The list of agreements drawn up by our country's partnership organization is the contract. Since the contract has provisions, profits and losses are shared according to shares, but the legal articles in the partnership section of the Civil Code make joint and several liability, which cannot but be regarded as a violation of the contract. Persistently adhering to this article that violates the contract and wanting the people to obey it, what about commercial bankruptcy? The examples and arguments advocating that joint and several liability cannot be canceled show that the provisions of this legal article completely lose their footing in legislation. It seems to be extremely clear. For this reason, we do not hesitate to use further broad citations to dispel private opinions. We earnestly request your association to truthfully submit this to the central administrative and legislative courts, in accordance with the codified laws of various advanced countries, as well as the prior customs that have been passed down in our country, and based on the principle of freely stipulating contract regulations, quickly amend Article 681 of the Civil Code, or even abolish it or order it to cease being used. We will listen to your wise decision. This is truly both virtuous and fair. Respectfully, Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Shanghai Municipal Miscellaneous Grain, Oil Cake Industry Trade Association, August 14th.

The Murderer in the Trunk Corpse Case Was Interrogated by the Portuguese Consulate Yesterday Morning 144

Audience Forbidden and Windows Closed During the Trial

The Two Murderers Were Neatly Dressed and Very Composed

The Portuguese Consul Expressed That They Must Be Transferred to the Macao Court for Trial

The murderer and accomplice in the trunk corpse case were arrested at No. 174, C block, Yifeng Lane, at 2:55 PM on the 14th by the patrol room together with the Japanese police chief and sent to the Xiamen Road West Prison for detention, as reported in yesterday's newspaper. The Portuguese Consulate interrogated the murderers yesterday morning. The details are as follows:

The Portuguese Consulate Interrogated the Murderers 145

The main murderer in the trunk corpse case, Bartolomeu Mitello, and his brother, the accomplice José Mitello, were arrested and detained in the Xiamen Road West Prison. The Portuguese Consulate formally interrogated them yesterday morning at 11:00 AM. This case caused a sensation in Shanghai, and many people were paying attention to it. Therefore, after 8:00 AM, there were many people on the road between Ma'erxi'ai Road and Lafayede Road going to the Portuguese Consulate to observe the trial, and many foreigners residing in Shanghai also went to the consulate to observe the trial, especially Portuguese nationals. By 9:00 AM, most of them had arrived, but unfortunately, the Portuguese Consulate forbade the audience from attending the trial of this case, so all those who went to the consulate to observe the trial were kept outside the consulate and could not enter. Although the courtroom could be seen, it was impossible to enter, so they could only sigh in vain. At 10:45 AM, William, the head of the patrol room's western patrol, had escorted the two defendants, the main murderer and the accomplice, from the Xiamen Road West Prison to the Portuguese Consulate. Dr. Sherve, the Portuguese Consul, questioned them about the case.

The Two Defendants Were Not Afraid at All 146

Before the main murderer Bartolomeu Mitello got out of the car in front of the consulate, he walked into the consulate wearing a navy blue Western suit and white canvas trousers. His brother was wearing a dark gray suit, also with white canvas trousers. The clothes seemed newly made, and his face also seemed newly repaired, so he was quite neat. When the two criminals walked into the consulate, they saw many people watching on both sides, but the two of them did not show any fear at all, and their faces were smiling, without any timidity. They walked in proudly. When the two criminals arrived at the consulate, they sat down in the defendant's seat in the temporary courtroom set up by the consulate. After forty minutes, Dr. Sherve, the Portuguese Consul, together with Inspector Leicester and Secretary Bai Laigai, sat up in the courtroom to question them. The Portuguese Consul wore a black suit and was very solemn.

The Municipal Government Sent Personnel to Observe the Trial 147

The victim in this case was indeed Chinese, not named Lu, but Zhang Cailian, a native of Guangdong. Her birth mother was in Shanghai. When she was young, she was bought by an American as a maid. She used to live at No. 9, Block B, Hainning Road. Later, she stole her master's property and escaped, and then lived on Wusong Road. She fell in love with the murderer Bartolomeu. When this case occurred, our Municipal Government paid close attention to it. Now that the murderer has been arrested and interrogated at the Portuguese Consulate, the Municipal Government specifically notified the Portuguese Consul in advance and sent Counselor Luo Panhui to the court to observe the trial with an official document. Because yesterday was the date for the preliminary hearing, it was only a temporary inquiry, and everything was waiting for the Portuguese Consulate to jointly interrogate the witnesses with the patrol room, etc. After the official trial is opened, another notification will be given, so Luo returned to the Municipal Government to report.

Defendant Hires Lawyer for Defense 148

After the two defendants were brought into the consular court, they sat silently in the defendant's seat on the right side of the courtroom, occasionally looking out at the spectators. The two defendants had hired lawyer Gu Lun as their defense attorney. Yesterday, Gu Lun also arrived in court, wearing his lawyer's robes. He studied the facts of the case in detail and repeatedly questioned the two defendants, but this was not audible to those outside the court.

Investigation of Evidence Begins First 149

At 11:30 AM, the Portuguese Consul Dr. Xue Erfo and the court clerk ascended to the bench together. The various documents and crime reports obtained by the police and Japanese police chief were read aloud by the court clerk, Bai Laijie. The two defendants were then asked if they admitted to the points mentioned, and whether they had murdered the Cantonese woman Zhang Cailian. During the interrogation, Bade Lie was questioned first, while his brother was taken out of the courtroom so that the two would not know what the other was saying. Each person was questioned for about fifteen minutes. At 11:50 AM, the second defendant was brought in for questioning. During the interrogation, because there were too many spectators outside the consulate and some were taking photographs, the Portuguese Consul ordered all the windows to be closed to isolate the court proceedings from the outside world. The interrogation ended at 12:10 PM. It was heard that the preliminary investigation revealed that the Portuguese Consul had ordered an investigation of the details of the murder and the scene of the crime at the intersection of Kunshan Road and Jiaxing Road that afternoon, as well as the collection of evidence, before scheduling another hearing.

Two Defendants Returned to Western Prison 150

After yesterday's preliminary hearing, Gu Lun, the defense lawyer for the two defendants, was said to have requested that the defendants be temporarily released on bail, with the understanding that they would be available upon request. However, the police and the Portuguese Consul both believed that the nature of the two men's crimes was too serious to be treated as ordinary cases, so bail was denied. After the interrogation, the two defendants were still handed over to Western Head Constable Williams, who escorted them to the Western Prison on Xiamen Road to await the formal scheduled trial. They were transported to the prison by car.

Police Summon Two Witnesses for Questioning 151

Zhang Tiansheng, the landlord of No. 15 Jiaxing Road, had vaguely heard groaning sounds when the crime occurred. Although Zhang Tiansheng did not know that the body of the murdered woman was inside when the box containing the body was taken out, he had witnessed the box. According to Zhang Tiansheng, the box was indeed carried downstairs from the upper floor of his house by a Portuguese youth on the 5th and loaded onto a rickshaw. Wang A'gen, the coolie, also testified that the box was indeed from the Shanghai Maru.

Eighteen Pieces of Evidence Arrive in Shanghai 152

Bandit Mistakenly Opens Fire, Killing Police Officer and Opium Addict 154

Opium Addict Follows Bandit Closely, Bandit Suspects He's Being Tracked

Police Officer Hears Gunshots and Investigates, Bandit Runs Out of Options

Two People Die Tragically After Successive Gunshots

At 3:45 AM yesterday morning, a case of a bandit mistakenly opening fire and killing a passerby and a police officer occurred near Xiangyan Bridge in the jurisdiction of the third precinct of the fifth district of Zhabei. The following is a description of the findings of the investigation:

Increasingly Degenerate 155

Xu Jinlong, 40 years old, from Yangzhou, settled with his mother, Xu Chen, in No. 4, Lane 147, Tiantong Road, Zhabei, ten years ago. At that time, Xu was a tailor, so his life was quite self-sufficient. Unexpectedly, he made bad friends and became increasingly degenerate, associating with hooligans all day long and becoming addicted to opium. His mother repeatedly tried to persuade him to change, but he refused, so she hated him deeply and immediately ordered him to leave and never return to the family. However, Jinlong not only did not change after this, but became even worse, living his rogue life. However, without any source of income, he soon went from being a rogue to a beggar. During the day, he wandered the streets, and at night he slept in the Shenjiawan area of Jiaxing Road, Zhabei. When he occasionally got a small amount of money, he went to the opium dens on Tongzhou Road in Hongkou to enjoy the pleasures of opium.

Following Closely 156

At around 3:00 AM yesterday morning, Jinlong had just gathered a few small coins when his opium addiction suddenly struck. He walked from Shenjiawan to Tongzhou Road, intending to go to an opium den to satisfy his craving. When he passed Jiaotong Road, he saw a person wearing a short shirt and pants running frantically in front of him. He thought it was someone rushing on their way, so he didn't pay attention. However, Jinlong was so addicted to opium at this time that he couldn't hold on for long, so he unconsciously quickened his pace. However, the latter had no intention, while the former was wary. When he approached Songjia Lane, the person wearing the short shirt and pants turned out to be a bandit. When he looked back and saw Jinlong following closely behind him, and it was difficult to distinguish in the darkness, he mistakenly thought that a detective was chasing him and decided to strike first. He took out a pistol from his side and fired a shot at Jinlong.

Two Shots to the Abdomen 157

The shot hit Jinlong's left palm, and blood flowed like a fountain. However, after being injured, Xu remained calm and took advantage of the fact that the bandit who fired the shot in front was turning around to run away, and tried his best to catch up, hoping to hold him back. Unexpectedly, the bandit also ran wildly. After chasing for a while, the bandit saw that Jinlong was about to catch up, so he turned around and fired a second shot at Xu, hitting Jinlong's abdomen. After suffering this injury, Xu almost fell down, but he still fled while injured. When he reached the vicinity of Hujia Wooden Bridge, he collapsed due to exhaustion. At the same time, blood flowed all over the ground, and he was barely breathing. At this time, Zhang Chonghui, a police officer on duty at post No. 23 of the third precinct of the fifth district on Linping Road, heard gunshots and was patrolling around. When he came to that place, he was discovered and asked Xu what had happened. Xu was unable to speak and only pointed in a direction with his hand. Officer Zhang then followed the direction forward.

Besieged on All Sides 158

At this time, the bandit had already crossed Jiaotong Road, passed through Songjia Lane, climbed over the bamboo fence, passed through Huachangli, and then Wuhua Road, and then Tianbao Road. The bandit had fired another shot along the way to show his power, so all the police officers on duty were able to find out the bandit's whereabouts, followed the sound to arrest him, and each took precautions. Before long, Officer Zhang had chased him to Tianbao Road. When the bandit saw this, he fled towards Taiping Bridge, but this place was guarded by Wei Xisheng, a police officer on duty at post No. 22 of the same precinct. Seeing someone running towards him, he shouted for him to stop and made a gesture of firing a gun. Seeing that his way forward and backward was blocked, the bandit turned towards Zhangjiaxiang Road and Linping Road. Unexpectedly, this place was blocked by Fan Yaoshan, a 30-year-old police officer from Anhui on duty at post No. 24 and No. 3026. At the same time, Officers Zhang and Wei chased from both sides, each holding a rifle, and fired a shot at the bandit.

Successive Tragic Deaths 159

Unexpectedly, it was late at night and it was difficult to distinguish things in the darkness, so none of the shots hit. Seeing that he was surrounded on all sides, the bandit was extremely anxious. He pulled out his gun and fired a shot forward. Fan Yaoshan was the first to be hit, the bullet hitting his abdomen. He fell to the ground immediately. Seeing that there was no one blocking his way, the bandit took advantage of the dim morning light and fled without a trace. All the officers and police of the third precinct of the fifth district pursued him without success. They immediately sent the injured Xu Jinlong and police officer Fan Yaoshan to the Hongkou Tongren Hospital for treatment in an ambulance. It was just after five o'clock. After Dr. Xu Chongen of the hospital performed surgery, Xu Jinlong died at 10:00 AM due to his severe injuries. The bullet in Officer Fan's abdomen was removed at around 11:00 AM, but his intestines were severely damaged, and his condition was quite bad. Unexpectedly, his condition suddenly changed at around 2:00 PM, and his body temperature also increased. Dr. Xu urgently injected him with a cardiac stimulant, but it was ineffective. At 3:00 PM, Officer Fan, who was injured on duty, also died in the hospital. The hospital reported the deaths to the police and the third precinct of the fifth district one after another. The bodies were transported to the coroner's office to await examination by the court this morning. At the same time, Director Wen of the third precinct of the fifth district had prepared a document to report to the headquarters and notified the other precincts to pursue and arrest the murderer and bring him to justice.

Triangular Love Affair Leads to Bloodshed 160

Zhang Jinfeng's Fickleness Causes Great Disaster

Chen Deyin Stabs Others and Then Stabs Himself and Takes Poison

At around 7:50 PM the night before last, a case of a triangular love affair leading to a bloody tragedy occurred at No. 8 Shenyuli, Roberts Road, West Shanghai. The truth is as follows:

Lodging with a Construction Worker 161

Zhang Jinfeng, a woman from Changzhou, is just twenty years old and has a pretty face. Because life in the countryside was difficult, she came to Shanghai at the beginning of this year and lodged with Chen Zhou, a fellow villager, at No. 8 Shenyuli, Roberts Road, West Shanghai. Later, she asked someone to introduce her to work at the Zhengda Cotton Mill. Chen Zhou is 61 years old and has a daughter named Xiaoda, who is only 17 years old and also works at the Gongyi Cotton Mill. Therefore, the two women spent their days together and were very close, and Chen Zhou also regarded Jinfeng as her own daughter and loved her very much.

Triangular Love Affair 162

In April of this year, Chen Deyin, a carpenter from Jiangbei, 25 years old, rented a berth at Chen Zhou's house since he had no family in Shanghai. Unexpectedly, he soon fell in love with Jinfeng. Jinfeng was just at the age of blossoming, so the two were very passionate and had secret affairs many times. However, due to his work, Chen often had to stay overnight outside, and he went to another port for a few days at the beginning of last month. Unexpectedly, Jinfeng was fickle and, during this period, had an affair with Yao Zilin, a waiter at the nearby Tang Yongmao Hotel. Yao often came to Chen Zhou's house and had secret affairs with Jinfeng. People were talking about it, and Chen found out about it. Thus, the sea of jealousy in this triangular love affair stirred up a huge wave.

Tragedy Occurs 163

Chen was consumed by jealousy and often thought of getting rid of Yao, but he had no chance to take advantage of. The day before yesterday evening, Chen returned from outside and suddenly saw Yao and Jinfeng sitting together and playing. He was furious. He secretly hid a sharp blade and said to Jinfeng, "The hotel room has been opened, let's go quickly." Yao heard this and cursed. Chen pulled out the sharp blade and stabbed Yao five times, one in the left wrist, one in each shoulder, and two in the back. Yao was immediately injured, bleeding and falling to the ground. Chen also felt resentful towards Chen Zhou for not stopping Yao from coming, so he turned around and stabbed her in the wrist twice. Seeing that he had caused a great disaster, Chen immediately grabbed a bottle of poison that he had prepared in advance (Chen Zhou said it was corrosive acid), poured it into his stomach, and then used the sharp blade he was holding to commit suicide, stabbing himself in the chest five times. Blood flowed like a fountain, and he fainted from the pain. Chen Zhou's daughter, Chen Xiaoda, was shocked and immediately ran to report to the police on duty. Police Chief Song Chengfa first sent the injured Chen Deyin, Yao Zilin, and Chen Zhou to the Red Cross Hospital for treatment. After the doctor applied medicine and bandages to Yao and Chen Zhou, he took them back to the sixth district. He also took the main characters, Zhang Jinfeng and Chen Xiaoda, back to the district together.

Both Sent to Court 164

After District Officer Jiang interrogated them separately, they were all vague and unwilling to tell the truth. Chen Deyin's injuries were severe, and the poison was taking effect, so his life was in danger. Yesterday, a document was prepared to transfer them to the local court for interrogation.

Zhou Miaoying Yearns for Her Son, Zhang Qu'an Disregards His Birth Mother 165

Miaoying Suffers from Poverty and Illness, Begging Qu'an in Vain

Believes That Zhang Xu Is Instigating and Has Filed a Lawsuit

Zhou Miaoying, a woman from this county, once belonged to the entertainment industry. She became acquainted with Zhang Shiming, the richest man in Nanxun, who was traveling in Shanghai. Zhang took her as a concubine, and she gave birth to a son named Qu'an. Later, Zhang's first wife died, so he married Xu as his second wife. After Xu married into the family, she treated Zhou Miaoying cruelly and did not allow them to live together. Zhou then left and took temporary refuge with the Qi family. In 1927, Shiming passed away, and Xu surrounded Qu'an, preventing him from meeting his mother. Zhou Miaoying then sued Qu'an in court, requesting support. At that time, Zhou was in financial straits and heavily in debt. Xu paid her 40,000 yuan and ordered her to withdraw the lawsuit. Two years ago, Xu married her niece to Qu'an, without seeking the consent of his birth mother. On the day of the wedding, Zhou heard the news and rushed there, but was surrounded and unable to see her son. Therefore, Zhou hired lawyers Yuan Yang'an and Zhang Zhirang to file a lawsuit in the First Special District Court against Xu and Qu'an to confirm their mother-son relationship. The first trial was lost, and the appeal also failed. A third appeal was made, and the Supreme Court ruled that the original judgment was overturned and confirmed that Zhang Qu'an and Zhou Miaoying had a mother-son relationship. This case has been in litigation for three years, and this newspaper has previously reported on it in detail. However, since the Supreme Court's ruling, Zhang Xu has continued to surround Qu'an, preventing him from fulfilling all the obligations of the Supreme Court's judgment. Zhou Miaoying believes that Qu'an's behavior is due to Zhang Xu's surrounding and instigating, so she still hired lawyers Yuan and Zhang to file a complaint in the criminal court of the First Special District, accusing Zhang Xu of instigating abandonment. There is a passage in her complaint that is quite tragic, stating that the plaintiff has been groaning in bed for several years, and the cost of medical treatment has been enormous, and she has long been equivalent to a cripple. Since last autumn and winter, her illness has become increasingly severe, and she has been in danger of death several times. Recently, she has also owed rent for more than six months and has been forced to move out by the landlord's lawsuit. Her remaining clothes and utensils have been sealed. The plaintiff was previously in critical condition and had no money for medical treatment, and she was forced to escape because of debt and had no way to escape. She sent a letter to Qu'an, begging him to provide relief and come to her bedside to see her, but Qu'an was still suppressed by the defendant and did not reply. She then sent a letter to the defendant, begging her not to restrict Qu'an's actions, but she still ignored her. The late husband, Shiming, was a wealthy man in Jiangnan, and Qu'an's inheritance was no less than ten million. He lives in tall buildings and luxurious houses, spending hundreds of gold every day. The plaintiff, in her critically ill state, not only has no money for medical treatment, but also has no house to live in. She is about to beg on the streets and die in a ditch. Such filial piety is lacking, and the abandonment of a person who should be supported by law is nothing more than the result of the defendant's instigation. Therefore, she specially requests that she be punished according to Article 43 and Article 311, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Code, etc. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Liu Yugui opened Criminal Court 8 and summoned her for trial. The original complaint stated that the defendant lived at No. 928 Xinchangli, Fujian Road, but according to the bailiff's report, the address was unknown and could not be delivered. Only Zhou Miaoying arrived in court. Zhou looked haggard and walked with difficulty. She arrived in court with lawyers Yuan and Zhang. Because the defendant had not arrived, the court could not proceed and ordered that the hearing be postponed.

Page 17

Five Assassins of Newspaper Vendor Zhou Yiting Arrested 166

Rivalry Due to Business Disputes

Municipal Police Bureau Also Arrests an Accomplice

Zhou Yiting, also known as Lao Wu, the chief newspaper vendor of the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway, was hacked to death with an axe by his enemies at 6:15 AM on March 22 of this year in Shanqingli, Er'jin Road. The murderer escaped from the scene without a trace and has been at large for half a year. The police have issued a wanted notice. At around 3:00 AM the day before yesterday, Hua Detective Shang Wu and Detective Liu Decheng of the Diss Will Road Police Station arrested five suspects, Wang Gengsheng from Suzhou, Xu A'bao (also known as Lao Kai) from Shanghai, Shi Xiangsheng (also known as Jinsheng) and Tong Baoxing from Hangzhou, and Yang Liangrong (also known as A'san) from Ningbo, at No. 193 and No. 207 Er'jin Road and No. 6 Tongzhou Road, and brought them to the police station. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court, where Judge Xiao Xiefen presided over the trial. Police Lawyer Zhang Tianyin stated the case, saying that there was another accomplice, Wu Shibao, who had been arrested by the Public Security Bureau in the Chinese area, and that the police planned to transfer him with an official letter. He requested that the hearing be postponed. When questioned, the defendant Wang Gengsheng confessed that he went with Xu A'bao, Wu Shibao, A'mao, and others at the time. He held an axe, and Xu A'bao also held an axe. They waited in Shanqingli. According to them, they were going to fight. After a while, Zhou Lao Wu came out of his house. Wu Shibao pointed him out, and he stepped forward and raised his axe to hack him twice, once on the right shoulder and once on the left leg. He then fell to the ground. Xu A'bao also hacked him once. Shi Xiangsheng was guarding the entrance of the lane. It was Xu A'bao who invited him to go. The axe was also brought by Wu Shibao. He received 62 yuan afterwards. Xu A'bao confessed that he did not know Zhou Lao Wu. He was invited to go by Gao A'mao. Wang Gengsheng was sent by him to go together. There were five people in total, namely Wang Gengsheng, Gao A'mao, Wu Shibao, Shi Xiangsheng, and him. When they saw Zhou Lao Wu, A'mao and Shibao shouted to attack. He then stepped forward and hacked him once. He could not remember where he hacked him. Shi Xiangsheng was the instigator. He had business disputes with Zhou Lao Wu, which led to accumulated grudges. He received 63 yuan afterwards. This matter had been discussed for a long time and they had gone three times but had not encountered him. Shi Xiangsheng confessed that he used to be a small newspaper vendor at Zhou Lao Wu's place, but he was fired by him. Later, he met his friends Xia Renliang, Pan Hongsheng, and Yang A'zai (also known as Liangrong) at the Laifeng Teahouse on Jielu Road. They talked about plotting to murder Zhou Lao Wu. He was joking, but they all agreed. Xia Renliang and Yang A'san gave him 300 yuan. He invited Wu Shibao to help. Tong Baoxing confessed that he was a newspaper vendor with Zhou Lao Wu, Pan Hongsheng, Xia Renliang, and others. He had no grudges with Zhou. He did not participate in this matter. The police lawyer stated that the defendant and Shi Xiangsheng were relatives by marriage, so they conspired together. However, Tong firmly denied it. Yang Liangrong confessed that he had been working at the Shanghai Electric Power Company for 14 years. Zhou Lao Wu was his prospective father-in-law. He knew Shi Xiangsheng because he often went to Zhou's house. He had not heard of the conspiracy to murder him. They were all falsely accusing him. After Zhou was murdered, he had stated that anyone who wanted to take over his newspaper vending vacancy would be the murderer, so no one dared to talk to him. Shi and others resented him and falsely accused him. The police lawyer also stated that Shi Xiangsheng had wanted to harm Zhou Lao Wu before, and he knew about it. He strongly agreed and urged him to proceed quickly. Shi Xiangsheng claimed that the 300 yuan was indeed given by Yang Liangrong and Xia Renliang. It was delivered in two installments below the Laifeng Teahouse. Judge Xiao ordered the defendants to be remanded in custody and postponed the hearing.

Red Swastika Society Provides Relief to Disaster Victims in Pudong 171

A Total of 1,587 Yuan Was Distributed

The Shanghai General Office of the Chinese Southeast General Assembly of the World Red Swastika Society dispatched Zhenwu Commissioner Wang Daoyuan and Niu Shang to Pudong on the 14th to provide relief to fire victims. At 3:00 PM, the names were called out from the roster at Yu Family Temple, and relief was distributed in order. The distribution was completed at 7:00 PM. The most severely affected five households were given six yuan each, totaling thirty yuan. The next most severely affected twenty-five households were given five yuan each, totaling one hundred and twenty-five yuan. Ordinary disaster victims were divided into three grades according to the number of people in the household, with the largest receiving four yuan and the smallest receiving two yuan, and the middle grade receiving three yuan. Ninety-five households received four yuan each, totaling three hundred and eighty yuan. Three hundred and twelve households received three yuan each, totaling nine hundred and thirty-six yuan. Fifty-eight households received two yuan each, totaling one hundred and sixteen yuan. A total of 1,587 yuan was distributed. There were still fourteen households that had not come to collect it. The Xinwei Relief Association and the Jisheng Association also distributed relief tickets at the same time to distribute the relief funds.

Jiande Bank and Jiande Savings Society 174

Since Jiande Bank moved into its building at No. 16 North Henan Road and commenced operations, outsiders have often mistaken it as an incarnation of the Jiande Savings Society. In reality, the Jiande Savings Society is a savings institution exclusively for members of the Chinese Jiande Society, while Jiande Bank is an ordinary commercial savings bank. The two have different natures and their economies are unrelated. Outsiders, due to the similarity in their names, have thus been led to some misunderstandings.

Expansion Plan of Shanghai Guohuo Company 177

The Shanghai Guohuo Company, located opposite the Hongmiao Temple on Nanjing Road, has been working on formulating an expansion plan since renting the building to the east. The outline of the plan is divided into five items: First, planning and constructing the facade; second, planning the interior layout; third, planning the necessary equipment; fourth, engaging in talent training; and fifth, preparing to expand the sales network. This plan has been handed over to the Business Development Committee for implementation starting from August 1st, with a fixed implementation period of six months, divided into three phases. The first to third items are to be completed within one and a half months as the first phase. The fourth item is to establish a foundation within one and a half months as the second phase. The fifth item, expanding the sales network, will be developed using the foundational strength built in the second phase over three months as the third phase. Once these three phases are completed, consumers in Shanghai who love using domestic goods will have sufficient convenience. According to the designers of the company, making Chinese people love domestic goods should be an easy task. The reason why this easy task has not made active progress amidst the advocacy of domestic goods is that the efforts to promote it have only focused on the promotion of slogans, without following up with practical steps after the promotion work. This will eventually enable the voice of advocating for domestic goods to gradually become a reality.

Over Two Hundred Street Vendors from Jiangyin Street Negotiate with Charity Group Yesterday 178

For the Station Road Vegetable Market Impeding the Livelihood of Jiangyin Street Vendors

Representatives Questioned the Charity Group, Who Were at a Loss for Words and Given a Seven-Day Deadline to Respond

Yu Qiaqing, Standing on the Position of a Fellow Townsman, Also Agreed to Assist Ningbo Vendors

All male and female vendors of Jiangyin Street, because the construction of a vegetable market on Station Road, planned by the charity group, namely the construction project, is also undertaken by the charity group, and it hinders the livelihood of all vendors on Jiangyin Street, therefore, since finding out that the group would hold a meeting yesterday, they voluntarily gathered more than two hundred people, mostly elderly women selling vegetables, together with five rotating representatives Yan Hongxiang, Fan Gongliang, Du Jinbao, Yu Miaofa, Xu Chunhua, gathered at the Shanghai Charity Group on Qiaojia Road in the city to negotiate, questioning the construction of the vegetable market on Station Road, which hinders the livelihood of all of Jiangyin Street, requesting to cancel the construction to stabilize people's hearts. When the vendors arrived at the group, the group's hall happened to have a clinic, treating the poor and sick. All vendors, under the maintenance of order by the five representatives, therefore the order was very good, gathered in the hall, after the representatives handed over the official letter, the person in charge of the group, Mr. Ye, came out to see them. When Representative Yan repeatedly stated the questions, the old female vegetable vendors all cried bitterly, scolded each other, and the order was slightly chaotic. Representative Fan tried his best to persuade and maintain order, but the vendors still demanded an immediate responsible reply and cancellation of the construction. Without a satisfactory answer, they would rather starve to death within the group than return home. The two sides argued until after twelve o'clock. The group, because the hall was gathered by vendors, could not have lunch. The representatives persuaded them to stand in the courtyard, standing in the scorching sun, waiting for the group staff to have lunch. The vendors were all hungry. The representatives paid for five hundred steamed buns to distribute to the vendors to relieve their hunger. The five representatives also gorged on large cakes to fill their stomachs. After the group had lunch, they reported to the Third Precinct of the First District of the Public Security Bureau by phone, who sent Patrol Officers Zhang and Sun to maintain order. Representative Yan asked Mr. Ye again whether there would be a meeting today. Mr. Ye replied that it was too hot to avoid the summer heat, and the board of directors would not meet. Representative Yan again requested a responsible and satisfactory reply. Mr. Ye replied that the charity group would not oppose you holding a meeting. I am responsible for convening a board of directors meeting to discuss it and will reply in one week. Patrol Officers Zhang and Sun also asked the representatives to persuade all the vendors to return home and wait for a reply. The five representatives feared it was a delaying tactic and insisted on a responsible and concrete reply before informing the vendors. Otherwise, they would resign from their representative positions. The two patrol officers advised not to resign and also reported to the Social Bureau and the Public Security Bureau by phone. The Social Bureau sent Fourth Section staff member Chen Lengseng, and the Public Security Bureau sent Patrol Officer Wang Ziqin from the First Precinct of the Second District, to the charity group, and comforted the representatives and vendors. As a result, they were allowed to wait for a reply in one week. Patrol Officer Wang and Section Staff Chen ordered Patrol Officer Zhang to inform the three temporary representatives to enter for talks. Xu Chunhua, Yan Hongxiang, and Du Jinbao were sent. As a result, Patrol Officer Wang was responsible for giving a satisfactory reply in one week. If it was not satisfactory, they could appeal to the Social Bureau. The three representatives were satisfied and told all the vendors before returning to Jiangyin Street. It is also learned that most of the vendors are from Ningbo. Representative Zhang Mingchang was sent to Mr. Yu Qiaqing, requesting to stand on the position of a fellow townsman to help his fellow townsmen and relieve their suffering. Yesterday, Representative Zhang went to the Sanbei Company and met with Mr. Yu, stated the reasons, and was promised by Mr. Yu to provide assistance and send a letter to Mayor Wu to cancel the construction of the vegetable market in Station Road. Therefore, the date of resolution should not be far away.

Kefa Pharmaceutical Factory Carelessness, Factory Director Sheds Tears: Fragrance Pervades 179

Kefa Pharmacy's pharmaceutical factory, located at No. 1568 Huade Road and Ningguo Road, purchased the land on which the factory is built. The factory building covers a vast area and is well-equipped, with separate departments for Western medicine manufacturing, chemical testing, and fragrances. In total, the factory has everything related to hygiene products manufactured in the factory. Its scale is the largest among pharmaceutical factories in this city. However, at 11:40 PM last night, a fire suddenly broke out in the fragrance workshop and warehouse. Thick smoke filled the air, and the flames roared. Because the workshop contained a large amount of perfume, fragrance oil, raw alcohol, and other materials, the fire spread easily, and the flames quickly broke through the roof, making it impossible to control. At that time, it was midnight, and the workers had already left work. Only a few staff members were on duty in the factory. Nearby residents and patrolmen discovered the fire and quickly dispatched patrolmen to inform the Central and Yangshupu fire brigades to send fire trucks to the scene to put out the fire. At the same time, the German factory director also rushed to the scene upon hearing the news. Seeing the valuable fragrances and other materials in the workshop and warehouse being burned, he could not help but shed tears. After the firefighters' best efforts, the fire was extinguished at 12:25 AM this morning. As a result, three fragrance workshops and warehouses were destroyed, resulting in heavy losses, which are difficult to estimate for the time being. When the reporter went to investigate and returned to the office, there were still embers in the workshop and warehouse, and firefighters were still continuing to put out the fire. The fragrance of the materials after the fire permeated the air and spread for miles. Afterwards, it was learned that the goods destroyed in the warehouse were mostly fragrance oils and floral water, while raw materials accounted for a large part of the workshop.

Huzhou Woman Lost, Waiting to be Claimed 185

Cao Guizhen, a woman from Huzhou, 19 years old, works as a servant in Shanghai. At 9:00 AM on the 13th of this month, she was ordered by her employer to go out to deliver a gift, but she got lost on the way back. She was found wandering in the French Concession with a gift box in her hand. The police found her and took her to the police station. According to her, her employer's surname is Jiang, but she does not know the alley or road name of her employer's address, and cannot go home. A card of Wang Xianzong was found in her gift box. The woman has short hair and is wearing a white short-sleeved shirt and trousers with blue willow stripes, barefoot, and wearing slippers. Detectives were dispatched to investigate, but it was difficult to find her employer's residence. The head of the police station ordered her to be temporarily kept and cared for while waiting to be claimed. If the woman's employer or relatives see the report, they can go to the French General Police Station in Lujiawan to claim her.

Four Banks Preparatory Treasury Issues Preparation Report 186

No. 189

The Four Banks Preparatory Treasury is jointly established by Yanyeh, Jincheng, Zhongnan, and Dalu four banks, specializing in issuing Zhongnan Bank notes. According to the treasury's issuance regulations, banknotes are issued with full reserves. Cash reserves are at least 60%, and guarantee reserves are at most 40%. An announcement is made once a week, audited by the auditors and accountants of the four banks. The following is a record of the Shanghai Preparatory Treasury's No. 189 announcement on August 12, 1933. Circulation amount of banknotes: 19,524,237 yuan. Total reserve amount: 19,524,237 yuan, including cash reserve of 15,764,637 yuan and guarantee reserve of 3,759,600 yuan.

Publishing Industry 188

Pre-orders for Lushan Zhi: Lushan is a scenic area in the southeast. Since Guling was opened as a summer resort, it has gradually become a world paradise. However, the mountain records have not been repaired. For nearly three hundred years, the history is unknown. Chairman Lin Liao-chao, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, and the heads of various academies, as well as famous figures at home and abroad, jointly proposed to raise funds for reconstruction. Mr. Chen Sanli, a senior scholar of Chinese studies, was responsible for reviewing the format and outlining the outline. Mr. Wu Zongci of Nanfeng was the chief editor, collecting thousands of ancient and modern books, many of which are ancient secret editions. It took three years and cost more than 50,000 yuan to complete the book. The entire book has more than 1.5 million words and 1,800 pages, and is printed in large Song-style characters on high-quality domestic Lian Shi paper, divided into two types: folio and octavo, for a total of twelve to fourteen books for the main records and six to eight books for the supplements, plus two cloth covers, which is very ancient, elegant, and exquisite. Now, the Shanghai Life Bookstore is specially entrusted to sell pre-orders. Detailed records of samples and pre-order methods will be sent upon request.

Humanities Monthly: The [Humanities Monthly] published by the Humanities Monthly Society on Qianjiatang, Lafayette Road, Shanghai, is well-known at home and abroad and has always been valued by the academic community. Recently, it was learned that Volume 4, Issue 6, has been published on schedule. The text in this issue includes Wen Yujun's [The Chinese Food Problem], which describes the current situation of food in China, the reasons for the lack, and the methods to solve it in the future without any omissions. Jian Bingjun's translation of [Germany in Transition] uses concise essays to describe the factions of German politicians and the reasons for the changes in great detail. Zheng Shixu's [Dr. Fujita Toyohachi, a Specialist in Transportation History, and the Bibliography of His Works] The original author is Dr. Koyanagi Sikita, who describes the life and career of the doctor and his influence on the academic and educational circles in my country. His works are also sufficient for reference for studying the history of transportation in the Far East. The notes include the secret manuscript [The Overthrow of Beidu], which was written by a Ming remnant, and records in detail the events of the Ming and Qing dynasties, which is still sufficient as a lesson for the current world. Wang Xiaoyin's [Huaxu Manlu] and Qian Luxiang's notes] have extremely valuable and interesting materials. Liu Guangyan's [Outline of the Almanac] has extremely valuable materials and civil service examination system], to the index of magazine essentials, totaling 2,101 items. The material is richer than before, and it is heard that ten issues are scheduled for the whole year. Domestic three yuan, foreign four yuan and eight jiao, including postage. All bookstores in this city are selling it on consignment.

China's Rural Economic Data: [China's Rural Economic Data] was compiled by Mr. Feng Hefa over several years, collecting no less than hundreds of materials. Important rural survey reports in China over the years are all prepared here. Most of the materials are not easy to collect lightly. In the autumn when the rural revitalization movement is flourishing, this book is of great help to those engaged in rural revitalization, rural education, and rural autonomy. Since its publication, it has been popular for a while, and the rural revitalization committees of various provinces and cities mostly use this book as a design basis. Purchasers of various schools and libraries are especially enthusiastic. Now, less than two months after publication, the first edition of 2,000 copies is about to be sold out. Less than a year after its publication, it has already been in its second edition. It is heard that the third edition can also be published within days to meet the needs of various schools to adopt it for the autumn semester.

Scientific Pictorial: The newspaper is organized by the China Science Society and printed and distributed by the China Science Company at No. 49 Jiaosi Road, Fuxu Road. The board of directors of the China Science Society in January of this year stated that since the publication of Science (Monthly), it has been seventeen years, and the texts published are all professional academic research papers. It is an indispensable publication for professional scholars to exchange knowledge and discuss experiences, but it seems to be too profound for popularizing scientific knowledge. It was decided to improve Science (Monthly) and separately compile and print a semi-monthly scientific pictorial in order to increase the public's interest in science and lay the foundation for construction. Since the publication of the first issue on August 1, the publication has been popular throughout the country and has been well received by all sectors. The second issue was also published today.

Letter 190

To the Editor,

In your newspaper's local news section on the 13th of this month, there was a report stating that local gentry in Beiqiao petitioned for the preservation of an ancient Tang Dynasty site. This is completely untrue. After investigation, the ancient bell tower in Beiqiao was contracted to the Zhu Bingji Construction Company for 7,500 yuan. Since construction began on June 20th of this year, progress has been remarkably swift. The project is now more than half complete. The claim that local gentry recently submitted another petition to the county government for funds to start construction is completely untrue. I am writing to request that you investigate and promptly correct this.

Sincerely,

Shanghai County Government

Ministry of Education Order on Free Adoption of Textbooks and Illustrated Books 199

The Ministry of Education instructed the Education Departments of various provinces, the Education Bureaus of Peiping, Nanjing, Shanghai, and Qingdao, and the Weihaiwei Administrative Office, stating that the review of textbooks and illustrated books should be uniformly handled by the ministry. The former University Council and the ministry have repeatedly issued orders to this effect. However, recent investigations have revealed that education administrative organs in various provinces, cities, and counties are still organizing textbook review committees and requiring all schools to uniformly adopt certain textbooks and illustrated books. This is inconsistent with the previous orders and Article 29 of the Elementary School Regulations, which stipulates that "schools should select and adopt [textbooks]." In the future, education administrative organs in various provinces, cities, and counties must not organize review committees to review textbooks and illustrated books that have already been reviewed and approved by the ministry. The adoption of textbooks should be handled carefully by the teachers in charge of the courses in each school, based on their practical experience in teaching, and no restrictions should be imposed. Otherwise, there is a risk that people may use their position to manipulate things in secret. It is difficult to describe the harm that this will cause. In addition to separate orders, the ministry urgently instructs that if there are organizations for textbook and illustrated book review committees in the provinces, cities, and counties under your jurisdiction, they should be abolished immediately. You are to take note of this. This order.

Important Proposals at the Annual Meeting of the Chinese Library Association 201

Funds and Savings Earmarked by Library Authorities

Regulations on the Minimum Budget for University Libraries

Libraries Should Establish Popular Departments to Develop Public Education

(Special dispatch from Peiping) Yuan Tongli, Li Wenxun, and other members of the preparatory committee for the second annual meeting of the Chinese Library Association have been preparing for several days, compiling information for attendees, and dispatching personnel to receive attendees. They have also requested the Ministry of Railways to offer discounted train tickets. The preparatory committee received many proposals on the 13th. All proposals must be organized in advance. The reporter obtained three important proposals. The various situations and important proposals are listed separately as follows:

Information for Attendees: (1) This annual meeting will be held at Tsinghua Scholar. The buildings and gardens of Tsinghua are magnificent and serene. Fragrant Hills, the Summer Palace, and other famous scenic spots surround it, making it a perfect place to rest during the summer. (2) All members attending the annual meeting will be accommodated and fed at the locations designated by the association (using the newly built dormitories of Tsinghua University). Those who wish to stay near their homes are also welcome. (3) From August 26th to 28th, staff from the reception group will meet members at the East and West Railway Stations in Peiping. (4) Continental Motor Company cars will be designated to depart from the station to Tsinghua University at scheduled times for members traveling to Tsinghua. (5) Members arriving at the station in Peiping do not need to carry their large luggage. The reception group will send personnel to take care of it properly. (6) Members attending the meeting should bring their own luggage, but it should be light. (7) Each member attending the meeting should pay an annual meeting fee of five yuan. The same applies to institutional members. (7) The reception group will print meal tickets for the members' meals at this annual meeting. Please collect them when registering. (9) The following discussion groups will be set up at the annual meeting. Members may join one or several groups and declare this at registration: (1) Library Administration Group, (2) Classification and Cataloging Group, (3) Library Funding Group, (4) Public Education Group, (5) Library Education Group, (6) Indexing Group. (10) Those who only purchase one-way train tickets and still need a certificate for discounted return fares should declare this at registration so that arrangements can be made on their behalf.

Important Proposals: (1) Proposal that library funding should be allocated by the competent authorities and libraries should have their own savings to avoid financial difficulties and facilitate operations. Submitted by the Nanjing Municipal Public Library. A. Justification: The establishment of libraries in China is nearly thirty years old. In 1930, the Ministry of Education conducted a survey and statistical analysis, combining general, specialized, public, school, and institutional libraries, totaling approximately 2,900. Although there may be some questions about these numbers, it can be said that their importance is recognized and they are becoming increasingly developed. However, in reality, not only are many libraries in counties and districts unable to carry out many tasks, but most of the established libraries in various provinces and cities are also makeshift and inadequate, focusing on one thing and losing sight of another, making it difficult to meet the demands of the people. The reason for this is the frequent turmoil and instability in the region, but the main cause is the lack of funding. It is inevitable that library funding will rely on the competent authorities, and the competent authorities are not entirely indifferent to this, but they are unable to do more than they can, or they are constrained by various problems. It is said that the annual budget of the Suiyuan Provincial Library is only several hundred yuan, which is extremely meager. If a way is not found to solve this problem, then there will be no progress in the future. Therefore, the competent authorities should allocate funds to cover the expenses of equipment, books, and affairs, rather than simply relying on the original public funds that fluctuate with changes. Libraries themselves should also have their own savings to serve as subsidies, to avoid being caught off guard by sudden emergencies. As the saying goes, "Long sleeves are good at dancing," and "Money is the mother of all things." Libraries are the central point of culture, the knowledge base of society, and the rise and fall of the nation depends on this. How can we be stingy with money and not plan for it early? B. Measures: (1) Competent Authorities: (1) Add an additional amount to the tax revenue and designate it for library use, following the example of adding a school tax when running schools in China in the past. (2) Allocate a certain amount or all of the fines to supplement the library. (3) Allocate surplus funds to supplement the library. (2) Libraries Themselves: (1) Add a budget item when preparing the annual budget and receive it monthly, depositing it in the bank for future use. (2) The proceeds from the sale of publications (such as books and newspapers) are deposited in the bank for future use (although this is done, it is extremely rare). (3) Charge a fee for those who come to the library for reference and research (not for ordinary visitors) and deposit it in the bank for use. The above is a proposal based on my limited knowledge. I hope that it is appropriate and that the public will decide. (2) Proposal to regulate the minimum budget for university libraries. Submitted by Gui Zhibai, a member from Nanjing. A. Justification: University libraries are active undertakings that require daily development. The equipment of university libraries in the country is mostly imperfect. If this continues, I am deeply afraid that the source of knowledge will be cut off and academic standards will decline. The reason for this is the uncertainty of funding, which is due to insufficient funds. Today, the Ministry of Education is striving to reorganize higher education, and it is appropriate for the conference to request the Ministry of Education to quickly stipulate a percentage of the school's budget that should be the minimum spent on [university] libraries nationwide, in order to seek educational efficiency. B. Measures: The conference should request the Ministry of Education to investigate the general situation of universities and their funding across the country, first formulate principles, and then stipulate the minimum standards for library funding and promulgate them for implementation. For example, the minimum standards for the library of a university can be stipulated as follows: If the annual budget of a university is more than one million yuan, the library budget should account for at least 10%; if it is below one million yuan and above five hundred thousand yuan, the library budget should account for 15%; and if it is below five hundred thousand yuan, the library budget should account for 20%. (3) Proposal to establish popular departments in libraries and promote circulation methods to develop public education. Submitted by the Nanjing Municipal Public Library. A. Justification: The increase in people's knowledge and the excellence of their education all depend on education. The general term "education" refers to schools. However, school education cannot be truly universal and is compulsory rather than free, temporary rather than permanent. However, libraries are the opposite. There is no distinction between classes, no matter how old or young, no difference between genders, and no regional restrictions. Anyone can enter the library at any time and choose books to read according to their preferences. Therefore, library education is public education. However, today's public and private libraries in China are not entirely the same. They follow the remaining style of藏書樓 [traditional Chinese library], although they also call themselves reading rooms, but the books they contain are mostly highly academic and suitable for scholars to consult, but not suitable for the needs of the majority of the public. The gates are heavy and lack a lively atmosphere, so they cannot be called public education. The public refers to all people and also contains the meaning of "popular". In 1915, in addition to issuing library regulations, the Ministry of Education also issued popular library regulations, with good intentions. As a result, the establishment of popular libraries has sprung up, and recently many are called public libraries. The books in this type of library should be simple and clear, so that readers can easily understand them, and practical. I still worry that their establishment is not complete, and specialized and ordinary libraries should also quickly plan to remedy the situation, widely implement circulation methods, and preserve the meaning of "popular", so that literate people have the opportunity to read, so that they can follow the rules when working and earning a living, and participate in politics and self-government. Their benefits to the country are not small. B. Measures: (1) Public and private specialized or ordinary libraries should set up popular reading departments in the library to allow people with basic education to enter and read. (2) All central libraries in provinces and cities should establish branch libraries to promote reading. (3) Mobile book cars or mobile book boxes and shelves should be set up (the Zhejiang Library and the Zhejiang Circulation Library have already done this, and our library is also planning to implement mobile book cars) for mobile reading. (4) More library agency points should be established to expand circulation. (5) More newspaper reading rooms or newspaper boards should be set up (our library has set up 40 newspaper boards) so that people can be aware of current affairs. (6) Library exhibitions should be held frequently to arouse people's interest. (7) More village libraries should be established to increase the knowledge of villagers. Although some of the above methods have been implemented or are already planned, the number is quite small. I sincerely hope that they will be widely promoted and effectively developed in the future. It is necessary to extend the use of books to the lower levels of society, then the power of public education will be greater than that of libraries. Is this appropriate? I respectfully ask for a public decision.

Extended Deadline for Issuing Certificates to High School Entrance Exam Failing Students 203

From the 15th to the 19th of This Month

For the convenience of high school students who participated in this year's entrance exam but did not complete all the required subjects or failed one or two subjects, the Municipal Education Bureau will issue certificates separately for temporary enrollment in schools and participation in the next supplementary exam. The deadline for issuing these certificates was originally set for the 10th of this month. However, as it is currently the summer vacation, many students from other places have returned home and have not been informed of this. Therefore, although the deadline has passed, there has been a continuous stream of requests for certificates. Therefore, it has been decided to extend the deadline by four days, from the 15th to the 19th of this month, to continue issuing these certificates. No further extensions will be granted after the deadline.

Municipal Education Bureau Bans Private Shiyuan Elementary School 204

The Shiyuan Elementary School located in the Shiyuan Lane of the Aier Cook Road on Tangshan Road was accused to the Municipal Education Bureau of having small and poorly equipped school buildings and extorting money from students. The bureau sent personnel to investigate and determined that the school was not operating in accordance with government laws and regulations and that its internal facilities were deficient. There are many schools in the vicinity, so there is no need to establish this school. The bureau has sent a letter to the concession authorities to ban the school.

Jianguo Middle School Continues to Recruit Students for Educational Subsidy Places 208

Chen Dezheng, the principal of Jianguo Middle School in Zhabei, has established educational subsidy places for poor students in the high school department to help students from impoverished families who are striving to learn. Students who are admitted to the school with a subsidy will be exempt from tuition and accommodation fees. It is learned that the school has already completed the entrance examination for the subsidy places for the past two days, and the admitted students have been notified by the school. It is said that this examination required preparation for social service, which was raised, and the supervision was very strict. Therefore, the number of students who applied and were admitted was not as many as expected. As a result, there are still five places available for the first year of high school and two places for the second and third years of high school. In order to fill these places, the school has decided to hold examinations at any time. Children from poor families with good character and academic performance can continue to apply to the school for the examination.
