[Marker] Tennis Tournament 211

[Marker] is a transliteration of Marker.

Enthusiasts Initiate

[Marker] in the Tennis Club is specifically responsible for managing the tennis court and assisting members with tennis practice. There are over a hundred [Markers] in various Chinese and foreign tennis clubs in Shanghai. [Markers'] tennis skills are generally of intermediate level. For example, Wang Wenzheng, who won the Chinese Open Singles Championship this time, and Qian Wensai, who won the Shanghai Grass Court Tennis Junior Singles Championship in 1931, both came from the ranks of [Markers]. Even the world-famous French tennis player Cochet also came from the ranks of [Markers]. In European and American countries, it is common to see athletes, whether professional or amateur, who have come from the ranks of [Markers], especially in golf, billiards, and tennis. The quality of [Markers'] tennis skills is closely related to the progress of members' tennis skills. Therefore, [Markers] are essentially coaches in tennis clubs.

[Markers'] Position In Shanghai tennis, there are quite a few [Markers] with excellent techniques, but the tennis skills of ordinary [Markers] also need to be improved. This is because [Markers] have a great influence on the progress of amateur tennis players' techniques. If [Markers'] techniques are excellent, amateur players' techniques will also improve easily. Especially since our country has no professional tennis instructors who can coach amateur players, tennis [Markers'] position is particularly important in China's tennis world.

Preparation and Initiation The reporter once chatted with Mr. Li Baojun, the manager of the Chinese tennis team, and suggested initiating a Shanghai [Marker] tennis tournament. It is now learned that Mr. Li is proceeding with this matter. The reporter met Zhang Kaisheng, a [Marker] from the Chinese Tennis Club, yesterday. According to Zhang, he is contacting [Markers] from various Western tennis associations to ensure that [Markers] from all tennis clubs can participate and strive to make this tournament a reality.

Realization Soon The prizes for this tournament have been donated by the East China Sports Company. The location for the tournament will be the tennis court of the China Sports Association at the intersection of Jing'an Temple Road and Hart Road. The registration fee is two yuan per person if borne by the tennis association, and one yuan per person if borne by the [Marker] themselves. Mr. Li is currently preparing for this matter, and it is expected to be realized soon.

Japanese National Swimming Championships Conclude 212

Four New World Records Created

Five Long-Distance World Records

Seventeen New Japanese Records in Total

Participants for Next Year's Far Eastern Games Decided 213

(Japan United Press, Tokyo, 15th) The third day of the Japanese National Swimming Championships began at 3:00 PM on the 14th. In the 400-meter breaststroke, which was most anticipated by the audience, Waseda University's Makino indeed set a new world record of 4 minutes and 46.4 seconds, breaking the 4 minutes and 47 seconds record held by France's Thalis. In this competition, Makino's time for 300 meters was 3 minutes and 32 seconds, Yusa's time for 200 meters was 2 minutes and 13 seconds, and Koike's time for 100 meters was 1 minute and 14 seconds, all of which were new world records. In addition, Kiyokawa's time for the 200-meter backstroke was 2 minutes and 35.8 seconds, female athlete Morioka's time for 300 meters in the 400-meter freestyle was 4 minutes and 27.8 seconds, her time for 400 meters was 6 minutes and 4 seconds, and Ms. Kojima's time for 200 meters was 2 minutes and 48.2 seconds. All of the above were new Japanese records. The conference concluded with praise.

(Japan United Press, Tokyo, 15th) During the three days of the All-Japan Swimming Championships, four world records, five long-distance world records, and seventeen new Japanese records were created.

(Japan United Press, Tokyo, 15th) The swimming athlete review committee held a meeting on the 14th to discuss the selection of athletes to be sent to the 10th Far Eastern Games next year. The results of the decision are as follows: eleven people were selected as the first candidates: (Freestyle) Kitamura Kusuo, Makino Masazo, Honda Soichiro, Miyazaki Koji, Sakaue Antaro, (Backstroke) Kiyokawa Shozo, Irie Minoru, Mizutsu Kentaro, (Breaststroke) Koike Reizo, Hamuro Tetsuo, Osaki Tamato.

Chinese Tennis Club Initiates Singles Competition for Members 220

Scoring System, Registration Deadline Today

The Labor Father Road Chinese Tennis Club currently has over fifty ordinary and student members. In order to promote members' interest and improve their skills, a singles competition for members has been initiated, using a scoring system to increase the competitive spirit. The registration deadline is today, and participation has been very enthusiastic. The details are explored and recorded as follows:

The competition method is to divide the participants into three groups, using a round-robin system. Each match, regardless of victory or defeat, must be played in three sets. The winner of each set will receive one point, and the loser will receive zero points. The person with the most points in each group will then participate in a round-robin tournament. The person with the most points in this tournament will win the championship, and the person with the second most points will be the runner-up. New balls will be used for the competition, and the cost will be shared equally by the two players in each match.

As of last night, the following players have registered to participate: Hu Xuguang, Wang Datong, Yuan Shilong, Chen Jinchun, Kuang Houfeng, Hu Zhongguang, Wang Wuchen, Hong Chuchun, Hou Shengxiong, Wang Bohan, Chen Chuanzhang, Xu Demin, Li Nan, Zhang Weiming, Qian Mingshu, Wang Jingye, Wang Zhaoye, Sun Yiqin, etc.

Publication of [Liu Changchun's Success Story], by Short Distance Running Master 224

Mr. Liu Changchun is a famous short-distance runner in our country. The three national records for short-distance running in our country were all created by Mr. Liu and have been maintained for many years. So far, no one has been able to match them. Mr. Liu also represented our country at the 10th World Olympic Games in the United States last year, opening a new era in our country's sports world and earning the respect of the Chinese people. However, how Mr. Liu succeeded, Mr. Liu's life experience, and the details of his participation in the World Games should be what those who care about him want to know most urgently. The Diligent Bookstore at No. 392 Labor Father Road, French Concession, Shanghai, has specially commissioned Mr. Jiang Huaiqing, a sports reporter for Shen Bao, to compile the book [Liu Changchun's Short-Distance Running Success Story], which details Mr. Liu's success and his experience to guide future generations and recognize Mr. Liu's contributions to our country's sports world. The chapters of the book are as follows: The Process of Liu Changchun's Successful Training (by Mr. Song Junfu), Chapter 1: Past Achievements, Chapter 2: A Bolt from the Blue, Chapter 3: The Times Make a Hero, Chapter 4: Thoughts on Going to the United States, Chapter 5: A Record of the Competition in the United States, Chapter 6: Talks on Returning Home, Chapter 7: Diary in the United States (one of Mr. Liu's writings), Chapter 8: Thoughts on Attending the Meeting (the second of Mr. Liu's writings), Chapter 9: The Starter (the third of Mr. Liu's writings), Chapter 10: Athletes and Marriage (the fourth of Mr. Liu's writings). Swap Longs Pay in $5.5 to $6.5

Yesterday, the gold market saw British and American silver markets both fall, and the exchange rate also narrowed. The price of forward silver on the Five Metals Exchange fell by 0.71 to 0.77 cents. The private telegraph silver price fell by 0.3125. American wheat was unchanged, and American cotton was slightly higher by 0.19 pounds per ton. Stocks fell by a little less than one yuan. The wool market opened and rose to $73.4, but although it rose, it still retreated. When the market opened, it initially appeared to be hovering. HSBC's listed exchange rate for the pound sterling narrowed by 0.0125, and the US dollar fell by 0.5 yuan. Later, it turned firm, probably due to the swap relationship. In the end, the banks were still firm. Reuters reported that the US Special Committee had completed a compromise plan for rural relief, which would reduce the amount of subsidies to farmers who reduced cotton and wheat production by 200 million yuan, and retain a small portion to repay their debts to the government, and strongly urged the government to stabilize agricultural product prices. The selling wind then arose. Shenkang failed in the article-by-article advertising help and was frustrated. In the latter market, it was initially low due to the large release of raw materials, but in the end, it was still stable. The price of cooked red was increased by $180. Silk and Tea: Zhejiang Autumn Silkworms Are About to Have Abundant Leaves 246

(Zhuji Autumn Silkworms Developing Well) After the silkworm eggs were collected in various cities and towns, they went through well. During the third sleep and wake-up period, they were affected by the hot and humid conditions, resulting in sleep loss and leaf stagnation. Now it has improved, and the large groups have third sleep and abundant leaves. The cocoons can be listed in the market in just over ten days.

(Quantity of Autumn Silkworm Seed Paper in Zhejiang) The Zhejiang Construction Department convened a meeting of directors of 15 sericulture counties and improvement farms on June 15 to develop autumn sericulture, unify silkworm varieties, and decide on implementation methods. The number of silkworm seeds produced and distributed this year was originally scheduled to be 350,000 sheets by the provincial silkworm seed farm, but only 250,000 sheets have been distributed. The seed price is 0.9 yuan per sheet, and it is estimated that it will be paid in two installments due to the economic panic in the rural areas.

No Hope, Therefore Embezzlement 253

— Lean Gull

In this era, the temptations of material things grow stronger day by day. Humanity's desire for all kinds of enjoyment is also becoming more intense and widespread. As a result, a beautiful vision of the future is piled up before every person who has not yet reached old age, causing them to pray and hope for it all the time. However, this society is now filled with all kinds of deformed developments and ugly darkness, which will make your very legitimate hopes evaporate and completely destroy your determination to strive. As a result: half of the people languish in boredom, and the other half easily become criminals in the eyes of the law. This phenomenon can be seen in the local news columns of various newspapers every day.

Yesterday, I was sitting in the criminal court of a certain court, and unintentionally, I heard the following noteworthy question and answer.

Judge: You were working well at the ×× Bureau, why did you embezzle public funds?

Criminal: (With a very sad and激昂 attitude) Because I knew there was no hope for my future, I had to use fraudulent means to satisfy my needs.

Judge: What are you talking about? If you can work diligently and do your job well, how can there be no hope?

Criminal: [Diligently work], [Do the job well], Haven't I been doing that for the past fourteen years! Seeing many newcomers who have been promoted through connections, one gets two hundred yuan, and another gets three hundred yuan, but as for me, I still don't even get a hundred! My precious youth has been wasted in this time of being constantly bullied and scolded. If I don't embezzle, what hope is there! (The voice became louder and louder, tears and sweat stuck together.)

Judge: Hmm... (hesitated for a long time) Alright! Embezzling public funds is still a crime, await sentencing! ...

After that, of course, it was several years and several months, but I didn't have the courage to listen anymore. I don't want to make any comments on this matter at all. In fact, I also dare not! However, I remember when I was a child reading about Ji Gong, whenever something unfair happened, he would always arrive gracefully. Moreover, he would often point to the sky and say: [There is a cloud of dark energy there, rushing straight into the sky, there must be something unfair happening, if I don't take care of it, who will! ] Then, he would really rush over and skillfully use his supernatural powers to handle the unfair matter in a fair and just manner, greatly pleasing the people. If Ji Gong really existed as a person, if he really had such supernatural powers, I think it would be impossible for him to live to this day. First, there is too much dark energy in the sky, and there are unfair things everywhere, which one should he take care of first? Maybe he knew in advance that such a day would come, so he extricated himself first.

Shenbao Amateur School Student and Teacher Reunion 254

— Qian Xu

The sun had just set below the horizon, and electric lights were not yet needed. In the elevator of the Eight Immortals Bridge YMCA, it was filled with people wearing badges all the way up to the ninth floor. These were the people from the five schools of the Shenbao Amateur School who came to participate in the conference.

Before the meeting, a dinner was held. In the cafeteria of the East Hall on the ninth floor of the YMCA, twenty-four tables were arranged around the room. The windows on all sides were open, and the gentle breeze swept over the cups, plates, and chopsticks on the tables, still projecting out of that side of the window: it seemed very refreshing. Waiters in white clothes hurried back and forth, and after a while, the signing area became crowded. One by one, people's heads moved towards each seat: Several people standing at the door kept uttering words of welcome, while at the same time every gaze was cast upon the badge of the person coming in. The students of the Second School stuffed their school publication | Dusk Clock | into the hands of every student.

Everyone sat down, and Principal Shi Liangcai sat at the table in the middle, smiling as he looked at his many students. The white-clad waiters began to busy themselves, sending dishes one by one to each table, but it was very slow, so Vice Principal Li Gongpu stood up and said to the many students in a humorous tone: "The dishes are coming too slowly, students, you can eat a little slower, don't eat too full and not be able to eat the dishes later." The students all laughed. The cafeteria was filled with what Principal Shi called [Sweet Air].

The conference opened,

The chairman, the principal, the dean, and the student representatives successively made many brilliant speeches, sincere, genuine, and affectionate, striking into the hearts of every student, and thunderous applause filled the space of the meeting place. It showed that the meaning of this conference was very great.

The chairman announced the start of the entertainment, and happiness ran onto the faces of the students again, replacing the solemnity. Then Mr. Mang Daling's story jokes, Vice Principal Li's Hawaiian guitar solo, the Shenbao newspaper's martial arts performance, and the movie "Mad Current" screened by the Mingxing Film Company, one item after another, one scene after another, the music vibrated the eardrums, and the performances anesthetized the soul, until the road back home, full of: joy, encouragement, gratitude, understanding.

Preserving the Status Quo 255

— Xia Ying

In the era of imperial autocracy, as commoners, under the [Vast Imperial Grace], we cautiously behaved as obedient citizens, living in peace and working happily, following the rules and regulations. We should not have wild ideas and do things that our predecessors had never done; even less were we allowed to be unconventional and establish our own unique style. Otherwise, it would be too restless and irresponsible, and we would be labeled as [Reactionary Elements].

Therefore, under such pressure, as commoners, we could only preserve the businesses already established by our predecessors and do things that others had already done.

Now, let's take an example, using the signboard of a store to illustrate:

Anyone who has been to Hangzhou knows that Zhang Xiaoquan's scissors are famous both at home and abroad. If we plan to buy a few pairs of scissors to give to friends, the difficulty arises; almost every street has one or two Zhang Xiaoquan scissors stores. Specially marked [Inherited for over two hundred years], [Only this one, no branches], which makes us confused. It is said that something with the word [Ji] is genuine. Upon closer inspection, [Near Ji], [Far Ji], [Da Ji], [Shu Ji], are all smoke and mirrors, all words with similar shapes.

There are also such things in Shanghai. The cooked meat store is always Lu Gaojian, and they are all marked with [Genuine] and [Old].

Others have worked hard to manage and finally have a store signboard with a [Good Reputation], and you effortlessly steal it and claim it as your own. I think this was tacitly approved by the government in the era of imperial autocracy.

If the imperial system continues, then the stores selling anything will have a uniform signboard, which would be a [Unified] and [Unique] thing.

The [Preservation of the Status Quo] from the Spring and Autumn and Warring States periods for two thousand years has created the current poor and backward Chinese nation!

Summer Heat Avoidance in Iron Bars 256

— Yi Qiu

Old classmate Mr. Li was arrested in the 19th year of the Republic of China due to political reasons and was imprisoned. He only regained his freedom at the beginning of this month. Yesterday, I met him in the park. Mr. Li said: [After spending three summers in prison, I never sweated profusely once. This summer, I just got out of prison and immediately felt the heat pressing down on me, which was uncomfortable. It can be seen that the ancient saying "A calm mind naturally brings coolness" is indeed true, because once you become a prisoner, you must be isolated from the outside world, and all thoughts are calmed down, and the state of mind is naturally peaceful.]

After hearing this, I couldn't help but marvel [Looking at it this way, we poor people don't have the qualifications to go to Lushan or Mogan Mountain, so it's better to go into iron bars to avoid the summer heat, which is also very economical. We don't even have to pay for room and board, wouldn't that be extremely cheap? ] I said this, and Mr. Li laughed.

Finally, Mr. Li showed me a [Prison Diary] and showed me a [Song of the Prisoner]. After reading it, I felt cool all over, so I named it [Song of Coolness], and with Mr. Li's consent, I recorded it for the readers of this publication, as a small cup of ice cream.

I will always be with this quiet iron window,

I hope my state of mind will always be like clear still water!

Every day, besides leisurely eating and sleeping, I enjoy the swaying green branches and leaves outside the window!

× × ×

I will always be with this quiet iron window, I hope my eyes will always be like pure white crystal!

Unstained by all the dirt in the world, always happily singing to the white clouds!

× × ×

I will always be with this quiet iron window, I hope my conscience will always be warm and safe, and all troubles will not approach me. The flowers outside the window always give me a secluded fragrance!

Character Sketch

A Glimpse of Yuan Hanyun in Pinghu 258

— Yi

Yuan Hanyun of Huan Shang occupies a considerable position in modern literary history. In terms of his family background, he is very similar to Chen Siwang Zhi, but his elder brother Ke Ding is not as good as Emperor Wen Pi. This is just my casual analogy, because when it comes to Yuan Hanyun, people inevitably think of Yuan Xiangcheng and his Hongxian episode. It just so happens that Wei Wu had a son who monopolized eight dou of talent. Hanyun is a bit like that, so I wrote this analogy. In fact, we don't want to dwell on the old accounts of Hongxian; we only feel that Hanyun's death is a very regrettable thing in the Chinese literary world, making people miss him endlessly! Therefore, we feel that the anecdotes of his life are even more precious. Below is a glimpse of him in Pinghu.

He went to Pinghu, I don't know what for. At that time, Xiangcheng had failed to become emperor and was still the president. The people of the whole country had negative feelings towards Xiangcheng. He went there by ordinary boat. In fact, Hanyun's personality was completely different from Ke Ding's. Hanyun fundamentally opposed Xiangcheng's claim to the throne and even bitterly admonished him in person; Xiangcheng didn't care much, but Ke Ding's enthusiasm for becoming the crown prince was even greater than Xiangcheng's, leading to the later results. Even if Hanyun went to Pinghu when the whole country admired Xiangcheng in the second year of the Republic of China, or even after the imperial system was actually successful, he would definitely not publicize it and take an ordinary boat. Therefore, at that time, he didn't necessarily go there quietly and secretly because the people opposed Xiangcheng. That was his magnanimity.

However, the local Pinghu Daily actually knew about it and specially published a special issue to report the news of [President Yuan's son Ke Wen arriving in the county], which stirred up the hearts of the people in the whole city. Everyone rushed to Donghu to see the boat Hanyun was on and catch a glimpse of the president's son's face. Who knew that they didn't see the son but saw the foolish state of his concubine's uncle, which attracted everyone's attention and made everyone laugh.

This so-called concubine's uncle was Tang Zhijun's younger brother. Zhijun was from Pinghu, and his father was a fruit vendor. The younger brother was still young and usually didn't wear long clothes. Hearing that Hanyun had arrived, he also knew in his childish consciousness that he had to go to greet him and couldn't go without wearing long clothes, so he borrowed a set of robes and jackets from someone and rushed to Donghu. Since he wasn't used to wearing long clothes and the set of robes and jackets were borrowed and didn't fit well, it was naturally inevitable that he would make people laugh.

Generally, all women have vanity! According to Hanyun's idea, he would spend the night on the boat to avoid a lot of trouble; Tang Zhijun insisted that Hanyun go ashore and go to his house for a while, thinking it was a great honor. Hanyun loved Zhijun very much and couldn't bear to go against his wishes, so he had to go ashore. But they couldn't live in his house, so they temporarily rented a house from someone. As soon as they sat down, a large group of people gathered outside the door. There were also many antique dealers who knew Hanyun's hobby and brought antiques one after another, seeing it as an opportunity to make a fortune. Even those who sold opium also came to the door to solicit sales, coming and going in an endless stream. The owner of the house knew that Hanyun wouldn't stay long and thought that if it went on for a long time, it would be terrible, and the threshold would be squeezed through; but it was inconvenient to say it to Hanyun directly, so he asked Hanyun's servant to express that he had a limited time to move out. The servant told Hanyun. Hanyun was very unhappy and immediately moved the whole family back to the boat. But he never said a word to the owner of the house.

After moving back to the boat, Zhijun again encouraged him to set off foreign fireworks, his idea being nothing more than to show off his wealth. Hanyun loved him and couldn't refuse, so he prepared. As soon as the news spread, many people came to watch. At that time, it happened to be under martial law, and County Magistrate Zhu Fubao sent someone to politely stop him. Hanyun immediately agreed. Zhijun and his mother were determined not to give up and still urged the workers to build a stage. Zhu Fubao was also a strong and upright official, and mistakenly thought that Hanyun refused to stop, so he immediately ordered twenty-four policemen to go to dismantle the stage; and gave a handwritten order: if there is any obstruction, no matter who it is, arrest them and report back. Zhijun and his mother had no choice but to stop, weeping and telling Hanyun. Hanyun was also angry and sent a telegram to Zhejiang Governor Lu Yongxiang. After the telegram was sent, Hanyun seemed to have forgotten about it. Without waiting for Lu Yongxiang's reply, he set sail and left Pinghu.

Free Talk

From Martial Arts Novels to Humorous Essays 259

— Qi Fan

Some time ago, martial arts novels were very popular. Their power was great. Some young apprentices in stores were fascinated by them and went to Mount Emei to cultivate themselves. The supernatural elements in martial arts novels are the pinnacle of martial arts, so those who try to obtain the highest martial arts always want to find immortals. The failure of martial arts novels lies in this, because immortals are not easy to find in the world, and their架空 always show flaws from time to time. Once they come into contact with real society, they cannot survive.

But martial arts works did indeed capture the hearts of the public for a while. Just looking at the number of types of books published and the畅销, you can know. Moreover, the film industry, which is good at speculation, has also produced a lot of martial arts and supernatural films for this reason, which can be taken as clear evidence. Moreover, the popularity of martial arts novels also has its inevitable reasons, that is, the public is thirsty for the appearance of this kind of warriors and heroes, even if they just look at it in books, they feel happy in their hearts.

When most people in society feel depressed, want to complain, and hope that someone will stand up for them, it is the era when heroes should appear. If real heroes cannot be produced, heroes in books will also be welcomed. In order to make the mind temporarily comfortable, people are willing to regard what is described in books as true. And modern China is exactly the time to demand heroes. Our soldiers can't beat Japanese soldiers, so we hope that a foreign country will stand up for us, that is, we hope for the appearance of heroes. We want to use broadswords and spears to fight against airplanes and cannons, just like hoping that there are flying swords and flying knives that can kill people in the air, that is, hoping that there are immortal methods that can win. But once it comes into contact with reality, there are obvious facts, so martial arts novels fail. Shanghai must sign a ceasefire agreement, and Beijing must also sign a ceasefire agreement.

At this time, a kind of humorous essay publication was produced. In less than a year, this kind of publication sprang up like mushrooms. It is not right to say that the status of martial arts novels has been replaced by this school of essays, but it is a fact that it has succeeded in becoming a popular hit. Most of these essays do not speak from the front, but take the method of attacking from the side, using metaphors and 暗讽 to express their feelings and vent their grievances. And the voice is also very weak, like a sob, not a loud cry.

Isn't this transformation from using broadswords to fight against cannons to 含诟忍辱 signing a ceasefire agreement? Since heroes cannot appear and immortal methods are not successful, then for the injustices in this society, there is only sobbing and resentment. This is the reason why humorous essays are popular after martial arts novels.

But will this slight sobbing and resentment have any effect? No one can be sure. Just like signing a ceasefire agreement is not a solution, it is necessary to wait for the second step of means. Let's see what will rise after humorous essays? Is it roar or surrender? Not only can the trend of society be seen from there, but also the future of China can be predicted from this.

Literati and Lice 260

— He Ru

Recently, I read Jia Yin Weekly and saw an article by Mr. Gu Tong, mentioning Chen Zhongfu. It roughly said that Zhongfu's original name was Gansheng, and his name was Zhong. He was from an old family in Huaining. He was known for his studies in his early years. He spoke sharply and liked to make judgments. He was impatient and intolerant of others, and was often not tolerated by others. He was unsuccessful in his travels to the East, and returned to Shanghai to establish National Daily with Yu (Gu Tong refers to himself), Cangzhou Zhang Puquan, and Nankang Xie Xiaoshi. The two of us热居 in the partial building of Changshou Lane, in charge of writing辞笔, without leaving our house. Our living habits were irregular. A robe of 縕 is what I rely on for life, using it to资其寒暑, and I have nothing to replace it with. I am often sick, and my lifestyle is very疏. My 寝 is worn out and cannot be released. I am脱略缓懒, and I am not diligent in捕讨. The 孙孙息息 have been around for thirty-five years." I think Bian Bin could not forget the lice, and his 擯弃形骸 was still not enough. He often worried about poverty and illness, and he had no far-reaching ambitions. It is said that Wang Jinggong once entered the court with Wang Yuyu. A louse climbed from Jinggong's collar to his beard, which happened to be seen by the emperor, who couldn't help but laugh. When he退朝, Jinggong asked Yuyu, "Why did the emperor laugh?" A Night Tour in Autumn 261

— You Guang

Autumn has already arrived, and the heat is no less than in summer. When the electric lights replaced the sun, I was still wandering on the road.

Dangerous? Danger makes people nervous, and坚张 makes people feel the strength of their own lives. Wandering in danger is very good.

There are still leisurely places in the concession, which are residential areas. But the residences of middle-class Chinese are hot, with eating stalls, 胡琴, 麻将,留声机, garbage cans, and bare bodies and legs. What is suitable is the outside of the residences of upper-class Chinese or 等洋人, wide roads,碧绿 trees,淡色 window幔, cool air, and moonlight, but there are also狗子 calling.

I grew up in the countryside and love to hear狗子 calling. At night, the distant bark is pleasant to hear. The ancients called [Dog sounds like leopards]. If you accidentally pass a strange village, a crazy吼叫 and 巨奦 jump out, it also gives people a kind of tension, as if facing a battle, which is very interesting.

But unfortunately, what I hear here is a叭儿狗. It躱躱闪闪 and calls very脆: 汪汪.

I don't like to hear this kind of calling.

I walked around and smiled coldly, because I understood that the way to shut it up was to say a few words to the管门人 of its master, or to throw it a bone. I can do both of these, but I don't.

It often wants to汪汪.

I don't like to hear this kind of calling.

I walked around and smiled evilly, because I had a pebble in my hand. As soon as the evil smile ended, I raised my hand and threw it, hitting it right on the bridge of its nose.

With a呜 sound, it disappeared. I walked, walked, in the rare silence.

Autumn has already arrived, and I am still walking. Calling is still there, but it is even more躱躱闪闪, the sound is also different from before, and the distance is also far away, and even the nose cannot be seen.

I no longer laugh coldly, no longer laugh evilly, I walk, listening comfortably to its very脆 sound.

Spring Warmth 262

— Zhu Daoyan

Ever since the several crop failures and last year's low grain prices, A Mao had grown fearful of farming. Especially as harvest time approached, A Mao's heart was filled with anxiety. Because on normal days the creditors weren't too pressing, but once harvest time arrived, they would find an excuse to urgently demand money from him.

Although he was anxious, he still held hope. Like this year's spring, seeing the green wheat seedlings in the fields, his heart always felt a nameless joy. By early April, the wheat ears were heavily laden and abundant. A gentle breeze swept by, causing them to sway as if about to fall. Seeing this, A Mao often muttered to himself as if making a vow: [This year's wheat won't be as cheap as last year's rice... I don't believe it, surely they won't deliberately make things difficult for us farmers.]

Harboring this hope, his former courage returned somewhat. He calculated inwardly: if this year's wheat price could be the same as last year's, selling at five dollars and forty cents per shi (a unit of dry measure), then sixteen mu (a unit of area) of land, assuming one shi per mu, sixteen shi would fetch more than eighty dollars. Although he couldn't completely pay off his old debts, he could at least repay some of the pressing debts, and there would also be some provisions for the family's consumption in the months to come. Thinking of this, a faint smile hung on his dark red lips.

Towards the end of April, A Mao was vigorously cutting wheat in the field. He bent his left knee, stretched his right leg back, arched his waist, hunched his back, held a handful of wheat stalks in his left hand, and held a sickle in his right hand. The sickle went to work on the wheat and moved back and forth along with the movements of his feet. The spring weather was erratic, but the sweat on A Mao's body dripped down like a network of threads, and his blue cloth shirt and pants were completely soaked.

After three full days of effort, A Mao and his wife had completely cut and threshed the wheat in the field. They harvested a total of more than sixteen shi. On the fourth morning, A Mao took someone else's dilapidated boat to the town to sell the wheat.

The boat stopped at the riverbank of a rice shop. A Mao walked into the rice shop to ask about the wheat price.

[Wheat is two dollars and eighty cents,] the shop assistant at the counter replied listlessly.

[What! How could it have dropped so much! Last year it sold for five dollars and forty cents!] Hearing these words, A Mao's beautiful hopes burst like soap bubbles.

[Look at how much wheat is on the market now. The current price is still good. When the large shipments of foreign wheat arrive next month, the wheat price will probably drop even further!]

A Mao felt a sting of pain selling at such a low price because the fertilizer costs alone amounted to one dollar per mu. But what could he do if he didn't sell? They still had to eat, and the debts had to be paid. Even if he waited a few more days, judging by the shop assistant's tone, there was no hope of the price rising. In the end, A Mao's wheat was moved into the rice shop's warehouse, and he received a sum of cash that was far different from his original budget.

Walking out of the shop, A Mao looked at the silver coins in his hand and said to himself as if muttering: [They really are deliberately making things difficult for us farmers!]

However, who exactly were the ["they"] in A Mao's mouth?

Autumn and Spring 263

— Lin Huiyin

Lu Xian one day found a self-bound collection of poems in a park. Its appearance and content were both very lovely. The next day she mailed it back to the loser at the address on a letter clipped to the book. After sending it off, she received only a short thank-you note, which made her somewhat dissatisfied, so she wrote another letter. But there was no reply. She couldn't help but be angered by the other party's arrogance. Angered, she couldn't help but write again and again, and she wrote four or five more letters in that way. After consistently not receiving a reply, one day she personally went to see the recipient. She saw him, in front of his door, but at first he denied that he was who he was, but then he admitted it and asked for her forgiveness. She felt the joy of victory, because his arrogance—she thought it was his arrogance—had really caused her too much grievance, so she repaid him with a mocking letter to end that curious romance.

However, Si Bin, the recipient, was not a person who would let his emotions rise and fall with other people's emotions. What he needed, he just needed, regardless of whether the person being needed had the same need, and Lu Xian was what he needed. So that letter of farewell could not stop his progress. He decided to write back. In that reply, he told her how he hadn't read her previous letters, and when he saw them, how he fell in love with her curiosity, coquetry, provocation, playfulness, and animosity; and when he saw her, how he fell in love with her hair, eyes, lips, chest, and calves.

By the time the letter was written, the sky was already beginning to lighten. He wanted to send it to her in person; because it was too early, he lay down on the bed and waited. But as soon as he lay down, he fell into a drowsy sleep, and when he woke up, it was already after twelve o'clock. He knew that she taught at someone's house from two to four o'clock, and he thought he might as well wait for her to return from teaching before going. So he walked to the first act setting of the drama in progress—the park where he had lost his collection of poems.

Once seated, he took out the letter and reread it. As he read, he felt that the letter was a bit shabby. Therefore, he eliminated his intention to hand it over in person; and if he handed it over in person, it would be embarrassing if she didn't read it, and it would be even more awkward if she did. But he still kept wanting to go see her. He looked at the big clock and it was only just past two o'clock. Two more hours! He stood up and ran around in the park. He was also imagining where his collection of poems had been lost. He was also wondering if her personality wasn't as beautiful as described in her letters! It couldn't be unlike, because affectation couldn't be so skillful; and even if it was affectation, wouldn't that affectation be very cute? Would she think he was going to see her? She would, he believed, because she herself was such an unyielding person; perhaps not going would disappoint and anger her.

Just as Si Bin imagined, Lu Xian, after sending out that last letter, was timidly hoping for his reply, or even his arrival. She felt that the letter had been sent out too rashly. His previous failure to reply always had his reasons, and she should give him a chance to explain and not just be willful in seeking temporary satisfaction. And this matter was created by herself, not by the other party's initiative. And, although at first there was only spite, now she seemed to feel a kind of indescribable affection spreading in her heart. She wanted to write another letter, but her pride wouldn't allow it. Therefore, for the past two days, she had been very lazy and had not gone to her lessons.

As soon as it was four o'clock, Si Bin left the park for Lu Xian's residence. At that time, Lu Xian was playing with a cohabiting child in the parlor. When she heard the unfamiliar knock on the door, she personally went to open the door.

[Oh, it's you! Oh, Mr. Si Bin.]

[Thank you, Miss Lu Xian. May I come in?]

[Please come in,] she paused and said, because she felt that the question was not easy to answer.

[You, Mr. Si Bin, you received my letter, I mean that...] Walking into the parlor, Lu Xian asked.

[You won't let me see the letter about you? I already received it, but you are really too stingy, Miss Lu Xian.]

[Because you are so generous, you can...] The ellipsis is a smile. (To be continued)

Talk

About Hiring a Wet Nurse 264

— Xiao Zhi

At the One-Month Celebration Feast

These are the opinions of guests at the Wang residence's one-month celebration feast regarding hiring a wet nurse.

When Mrs. Wang smilingly brought out her firstborn young master, everyone naturally praised him with admiring words like "So fair and tender, so cute." Mrs. Wang then sat on the host's seat, below Mr. Wang.

[Is your milk supply good?] Old Man Chen, with a handful of long whiskers on his chin, was the first to ask Mrs. Wang. Mrs. Wang blushed red, bit her lip, and did not answer Old Man Chen, only glancing at Mr. Wang. Mr. Wang readily said:

[We hired a wet nurse. Our own milk has not yet been given to the child.]

[This is not very good. If the child only drinks the wet nurse's milk, the child's personality will be like the wet nurse's when he grows up,] Old Man Chen said, feeling the issue of racial constitution, expressing his disapproval.

[Unbuttoning clothes to breastfeed the child is quite embarrassing...] Mrs. Wang explained bashfully. [I often heard my classmates say before that using one's own milk to feed the child is very easy to destroy one's youth.]

[This makes a lot of sense.] Most of the guests expressed their sympathy, including Mr. Wang. Only Old Man Chen put his left arm on the back of the chair, looked up, his eyes fixed on the ceiling, his right hand constantly stroking his beard, looking as if he was very sentimental.

[Actually, these are all irrelevant. Having money can certainly hire a wet nurse to [help out], and it is said that it can also maintain the beauty of the mother's youth; but we should also consider at the same time: the wet nurse absolutely does not have milk to sell if she does not have children herself. In such a matter, we can clearly see: the wet nurse sells her milk and starves her own child's stomach; then, the rich buy the wet nurse's milk, which is equivalent to taking, robbing, and plundering the wet nurse's child's food, and this little life is in danger of starving to death and being destroyed!...] My words welled up to my throat several times, but were always swallowed down into my stomach by the big fish and meat.

I Deceived Her! 265

— Xin

[Second Miss, I should always find a way to find a way to make a living,] the maid from the Wu family next door said to me:

[Yes, Ah Chen, your mistress is really too harsh on you today,] I replied to him with great sympathy and pity.

Seeing my sympathy, he continued:

[Second Miss, look, today I accidentally broke a bowl, and she scolded me [White Tiger] [Troublemaker], told me to get out, and said that with money, it's not hard to find a clumsy maid like me...]

[Alas! Ah Chen, earning money is indeed too difficult. Now you really have no other way but to work as a maid for others; for the sake of money, I think you should endure it and keep working!]

Ah Chen still looked mournful, so I said again:

[You need to know that it's difficult to work for people everywhere!]

[Second Miss, your family's Ah Si is also a maid like me. When he makes a small mistake, you don't scold him at all. I...] He sobbed and cried.

[Ah Chen, I would also be happy for you to come to my house to work, but... but Ah Si doesn't have any bad habits, how can we dismiss him?]

I said hesitatingly, not wanting to disappoint him:

[Think about it, Second Miss, they simply treat me like a thief, locking the doors in and out; when I break something, they even scold me for things from previous years, shouting [Get out] again and again, alas, how can I live this kind of life?] His tears welled up like a spring.

[Ah Chen, slowly wait, wait for the arrival of opportunity,] I said to him very cleverly: [Ah Chen, suffer a little bit, suffer for ten or eight years, accumulate some money, and then you will be out of your misery.]

[Ah Chen, Ah Chen,] a voice from outside came in, which was clearly the voice of his mistress.

Ah Chen wiped his tears and ran back in a hurry. I stared blankly at his retreating figure; I thought, I have been clever again, I deceived her!

Street Night Scene 266

— Guanying

Night enveloped the earth, and New Year's lanterns were already flickering in the streets. The fiery atmosphere of the daytime had long been blown by the evening breeze to the ends of the earth. People in the summer, except for the working class, mostly were accustomed to resting during the day and coming out at night. At this moment, as the night was just beginning, it was precisely when they began to be active. The night of the city was originally full of mystery, and the romance of the imperial daughters in a corner of Hongkou added a bit of spring color. Under the dim lights, small groups of wooden clogs-wearing women, heavily made up, leaned against doors, smiling and selling their charms to people. No matter how grand the imperial ambition was, it could not cover the shame and sorrow deep in the hearts of the daughters.

Groups of three or five European sailors constantly came to this mysterious corner to pursue pleasure. The mingling of foreign emotions stirred a deep feeling in my heart. Cinemas, dance halls... were the places where they pursued pleasure and roamed about. The temptation of flesh, the allure of colors, the ancient costumes of large kimonos, wrapped around slender figures, no matter how heroic Western nations were, they could not resist their soft and charming teasing. So they embraced, danced, and in their crimson lips, Eastern and Western cultures were exchanged.

Short, waddling imperial warriors walked in groups on the streets. The sound of leather shoes, accompanied by arrogant expressions and high spirits, moved forward. I could not help but recall the events of January 28th and express a gnashing of teeth and angry gaze at them.

Next door was a Tokyo hotel. The New Year's lanterns outside reflected the pale green lights on the upper floor. Amidst the leisurely music and dance, the imperial daughters' songs also rose up, only stopping when the night was deep and quiet.

Ugh! Bang! An ambulance drove from afar and stopped next to a hospital across the street. Was it suicide? Revenge killing? A car accident? The lives of city people were so uncertain!
